//REGION Vector Math Helpers
// Multiply a vector by a scalar
QRY
QRY_VectorMult((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_Scalar)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorMult((REAL)_XD, (REAL)_YD, (REAL)_ZD)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_VectorMult(_XD, _YD, _ZD);

QRY
QRY_VectorMult((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_Scalar)
AND
RealProduct(_XA, _Scalar, (REAL)_XD)
AND
RealProduct(_YA, _Scalar, (REAL)_YD)
AND
RealProduct(_ZA, _Scalar, (REAL)_ZD)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_VectorMult(_XD, _YD, _ZD);

// Calculate the vector A->B
QRY
QRY_VectorAB((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_XB, (REAL)_YB, (REAL)_ZB)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorAB((REAL)_XD, (REAL)_YD, (REAL)_ZD)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_VectorAB(_XD, _YD, _ZD);

QRY
QRY_VectorAB((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_XB, (REAL)_YB, (REAL)_ZB)
AND
RealSubtract(_XB, _XA, (REAL)_XD)
AND
RealSubtract(_YB, _YA, (REAL)_YD)
AND
RealSubtract(_ZB, _ZA, (REAL)_ZD)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_VectorAB(_XD, _YD, _ZD);

// Calculate the position vector along axis A->B of length Distance
QRY
QRY_VectorABByDistance((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_XB, (REAL)_YB, (REAL)_ZB, (REAL)_Distance)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorABByDistance((REAL)_XN, (REAL)_YN, (REAL)_ZN)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_VectorABByDistance(_XN, _YN, _ZN);

QRY
QRY_VectorABByDistance((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_XB, (REAL)_YB, (REAL)_ZB, (REAL)_Distance)
AND
QRY_GetReal3SqrDistance(_XA, _YA, _ZA, _XB, _YB, _ZB)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_GetReal3SqrDistance((REAL)_ABSq)
AND
RealSqrRoot(_ABSq, (REAL)_ABDist)
AND
QRY_VectorAB(_XA, _YA, _ZA, _XB, _YB, _ZB)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorAB((REAL)_XD, (REAL)_YD, (REAL)_ZD)
AND
RealDivide(1.0, _ABDist, (REAL)_Quotient)
AND
RealProduct(_Quotient, _Distance, _Multiplier)
AND
QRY_VectorMult(_XD, _YD, _ZD, _Multiplier)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorMult((REAL)_XDN, (REAL)_YDN, (REAL)_ZDN)
AND
RealSum(_XDN, _XA, (REAL)_XN)
AND
RealSum(_YDN, _YA, (REAL)_YN)
AND
RealSum(_ZDN, _ZA, (REAL)_ZN)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_VectorABByDistance(_XN, _YN, _ZN);

// Calculate the position vector Ratio along axis A->B
QRY
QRY_VectorABByRatio((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_XB, (REAL)_YB, (REAL)_ZB, (REAL)_Ratio)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorABByRatio((REAL)_XN, (REAL)_YN, (REAL)_ZN)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_VectorABByRatio(_XN, _YN, _ZN);

QRY
QRY_VectorABByRatio((REAL)_XA, (REAL)_YA, (REAL)_ZA, (REAL)_XB, (REAL)_YB, (REAL)_ZB, (REAL)_Ratio)
AND
QRY_VectorAB(_XA, _YA, _ZA, _XB, _YB, _ZB)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorAB((REAL)_XD, (REAL)_YD, (REAL)_ZD)
AND
QRY_VectorMult(_XD, _YD, _ZD, _Ratio)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_VectorMult((REAL)_XDN, (REAL)_YDN, (REAL)_ZDN)
AND
RealSum(_XDN, _XA, (REAL)_XN)
AND
RealSum(_YDN, _YA, (REAL)_YN)
AND
RealSum(_ZDN, _ZA, (REAL)_ZN)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_VectorABByRatio(_XN, _YN, _ZN);
//END_REGION

//REGION Trig Functions
// Calculate the sine value of an angle in degrees
QRY
QRY_Sine((REAL)_Angle)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_Sine((REAL)_Value)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_Sine(_Value);

QRY
QRY_Sine((REAL)_Angle)
AND
RealProduct(_Angle, 10.0, (REAL)_MultAngle)
AND
RealToInteger(_MultAngle, (INTEGER)_IntAngle)
AND
DB_SineValue(_IntAngle, (REAL)_Value)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_Sine(_Value);

// Calculate the cosine value of an angle in degrees
QRY
QRY_Cosine((REAL)_Angle)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_Cosine((REAL)_Value)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_Cosine(_Value);

QRY
QRY_Cosine((REAL)_Angle)
AND
RealSum(_Angle, 90.0, (REAL)_CosAngle)
AND
QRY_Sine(_CosAngle)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_Sine((REAL)_Value)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_Cosine(_Value);

// Calculate 2D unit vector at angle in degrees
QRY
QRY_UnitVectorAtAngle((REAL)_Angle)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_UnitVectorAtAngle((REAL)_X, (REAL)_Z)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_UnitVectorAtAngle(_X, _Z);

QRY
QRY_UnitVectorAtAngle((REAL)_Angle)
AND
QRY_Sine(_Angle)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_Sine((REAL)_X)
AND
QRY_Cosine(_Angle)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_Cosine((REAL)_Z)
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_UnitVectorAtAngle(_X, _Z);

// Test if 2D line A->B intersects with C->D
// Note that this does not return the point of
// intersection, in large part because to do so
// comes with potential divide by zero issues.
QRY
QRY_LinesIntersect((REAL)_AX, (REAL)_AZ, (REAL)_BX, (REAL)_BZ, (REAL)_CX, (REAL)_CZ, (REAL)_DX, (REAL)_DZ)
AND
DB_QRYRTN_LinesIntersect((INTEGER)_Intersects)
THEN
NOT DB_QRYRTN_LinesIntersect(_Intersects);

QRY
QRY_LinesIntersect((REAL)_AX, (REAL)_AZ, (REAL)_BX, (REAL)_BZ, (REAL)_CX, (REAL)_CZ, (REAL)_DX, (REAL)_DZ)
AND
RealSubtract(_BX, _AX, (REAL)_dX0)
AND
RealSubtract(_DX, _CX, (REAL)_dX1)
AND
RealSubtract(_BZ, _AZ, (REAL)_dZ0)
AND
RealSubtract(_DZ, _CZ, (REAL)_dZ1)
AND
RealSubtract(_DX, _AX, (REAL)_dXDA)
AND
RealSubtract(_DZ, _AZ, (REAL)_dZDA)
AND
RealSubtract(_DX, _BX, (REAL)_dXDB)
AND
RealSubtract(_DZ, _BZ, (REAL)_dZDB)
AND
RealSubtract(_BX, _CX, (REAL)_dXBC)
AND
RealSubtract(_BZ, _CZ, (REAL)_dZBC)
AND
RealSubtract(_BX, _DX, (REAL)_dXBD)
AND
RealSubtract(_BZ, _DZ, (REAL)_dZBD)
AND
RealProduct(_dZ1, _dXDA, (REAL)_p00)
AND
RealProduct(_dZ1, _dXDB, (REAL)_p10)
AND
RealProduct(_dX1, _dZDA, (REAL)_p01)
AND
RealProduct(_dX1, _dZDB, (REAL)_p11)
AND
RealProduct(_dZ0, _dXBC, (REAL)_p20)
AND
RealProduct(_dZ0, _dXBD, (REAL)_p30)
AND
RealProduct(_dX0, _dZBC, (REAL)_p21)
AND
RealProduct(_dX0, _dZBD, (REAL)_p31)
AND
RealSubtract(_p00, _p01, (REAL)_p0)
AND
RealSubtract(_p10, _p11, (REAL)_p1)
AND
RealSubtract(_p20, _p21, (REAL)_p2)
AND
RealSubtract(_p30, _p31, (REAL)_p3)
AND
RealProduct(_p0, _p1, (REAL)_c0)
AND
RealProduct(_p2, _p3, (REAL)_c1)
THEN
PROC_LinesIntersectCheckSigns(_c0, _c1);

PROC
PROC_LinesIntersectCheckSigns((REAL)_c0, (REAL)_c1)
AND
NOT _c0 > 0.0
AND
NOT _c1 > 0.0
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_LinesIntersect(1);

PROC
PROC_LinesIntersectCheckSigns((REAL)_c0, (REAL)_c1)
AND
_c0 > 0.0
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_LinesIntersect(0);

PROC
PROC_LinesIntersectCheckSigns((REAL)_c0, (REAL)_c1)
AND
_c1 > 0.0
THEN
DB_QRYRTN_LinesIntersect(0);
//END_REGION
EXITSECTION

ENDEXITSECTION
